### <a id="inductive-types-h-s-p-and-v">Inductive Types H, S, P, and V</a>

This section presents the [UALib.Varieties.Varieties][] module of the [Agda Universal Algebra Library][].

Fix a signature 𝑆, let 𝒦 be a class of 𝑆-algebras, and define

* H 𝒦 = algebras isomorphic to a homomorphic image of a members of 𝒦;
* S 𝒦 = algebras isomorphic to a subalgebra of a member of 𝒦;
* P 𝒦 = algebras isomorphic to a product of members of 𝒦.

A straight-forward verification confirms that H, S, and P are **closure operators** (expansive, monotone, and idempotent).  A class 𝒦 of 𝑆-algebras is said to be *closed under the taking of homomorphic images* provided `H 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦`. Similarly, 𝒦 is *closed under the taking of subalgebras* (resp., *arbitrary products*) provided `S 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦` (resp., `P 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦`).

An algebra is a homomorphic image (resp., subalgebra; resp., product) of every algebra to which it is isomorphic. Thus, the class `H 𝒦` (resp., `S 𝒦`; resp., `P 𝒦`) is closed under isomorphism.

The operators H, S, and P can be composed with one another repeatedly, forming yet more closure operators.

<!-- If C₁ and C₂ are closure operators on classes of structures, let us say that C₁ ≤ C₂ if for every class 𝒦 we have C₁(𝒦) ⊆ C₂(𝒦). -->

A **variety** is a class 𝒦 of algebras in a fixed signature that is closed under the taking of homomorphic images (H), subalgebras (S), and arbitrary products (P).  That is, 𝒦 is a variety if and only if `H S P 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦`.

This module defines what we have found to be the most useful inductive types representing the closure operators H, S, and P. Separately, we define the inductive type `V` for simultaneously representing closure under `H`, `S`, and `P`.

<!-- ; consequently, we expect `V 𝒦 ≡ H (S (P 𝒦))` to hold for each class 𝒦 of algebras of a fixed signature. classes of algebras that are closed under H, S, P, and V ≡ HSP. -->

#### <a id="homomorphic-closure">Homomorphism closure</a>

We define the inductive type `H` to represent classes of algebras that include all homomorphic images of algebras in the class; i.e., classes that are closed under the taking of homomorphic images.

<pre class="Agda">

<!-- We say that a class 𝒦 is **closed under** `H` (or `H`-**closed**) provided `H 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦`. -->

--------------------------------

#### <a id="subalgebra-closure">Subalgebra closure</a>

The most useful inductive type that we have found for representing classes of algebras that are closed under the taking of subalgebras as an inductive type.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="3520" class="Comment">--Closure wrt S</a>
<a id="3536" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="S"></a><a id="3541" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3541" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="3543" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3544" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3544" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="3546" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3546" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="3548" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3550" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="3558" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="3560" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3560" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="3562" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3564" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="3569" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3570" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="3578" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3544" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="3580" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="3581" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3583" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3584" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1698" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="3587" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3544" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="3588" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="3591" class="Symbol">:</a>
 <a id="3594" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="3599" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3600" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="3608" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3609" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3544" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="3611" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="3613" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3546" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="3614" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3616" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="3617" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3619" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3620" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1698" class="Function">ov</a><a id="3622" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3623" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3544" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="3625" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="3627" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3546" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="3628" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="3631" class="Keyword">where</a>

href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3560" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

</pre>

<!-- A class 𝒦 is **closed under** `S` (or `S`-**closed**) provided `S 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦` -->

-----------------------------------------

#### <a id="product-closure">Product closure</a>

The most useful inductive type that we have found for representing classes of algebras closed under arbitrary products is the following. 

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="4323" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="P"></a><a id="4328" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4328" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="4330" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4331" <a id="4351" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="4356" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4357" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="4365" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4331" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="4367" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="4368" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="4370" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1698" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="4373" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4331" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="4374" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="4377" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4379" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="4384" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4385" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="4393" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4394" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4331" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="4396" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="4398" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4333" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="4399" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4401" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258"   <a id="P.prodw"></a><a id="4708" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4708" class="InductiveConstructor">prodw</a>  <a id="4715" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4717" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4718" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="4772" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4774" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4347" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="4775" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4777" class="Symbol">→</a> <a </pre>

<!-- A class 𝒦 is **closed under** `P` (or `P`-**closed**) provided `P 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦`. -->

-----------------------------------------------

#### <a id="variety-closure">Varietal closure</a>

A class 𝒦 of 𝑆-algebras is called a **variety** if it is closed under each of the closure operators H, S, and P introduced above; the corresponding closure operator is often denoted 𝕍, but we will typically denote it by `V`.

Thus, if 𝒦 is a class of 𝑆-algebras, then the **variety generated by** 𝒦 is denoted by `V 𝒦` and defined to be the smallest class that contains 𝒦 and is closed under `H`, `S`, and `P`.

We now define `V` as an inductive type.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="5598" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="V"></a><a id="5603" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5603" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="5605" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5606" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5606" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5608" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5608" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="5610" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5612" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="5620" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="5622" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5622" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="5624" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5626" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="5631" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5632" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5640" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5606" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5642" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5643" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="5645" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1698" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="5648" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5606" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5649" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="5652" class="Symbol">:</a>
 <a id="5655" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="5660" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5661" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5669" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5670" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5606" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5672" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="5674" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5608" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="5675" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5677" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5678" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="5680" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1698" class="Function">ov</a><a id="5682" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5683" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5606" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5685" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="5687" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5608" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="5688" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="5691" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="V.vbase"></a><a id="5699" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5699" class="InductiveConstructor">vbase</a>  <a id="5706" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5708" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5709" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5709" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5711" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5713" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5721" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5606" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5723" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5724" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5726" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5728" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5709" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5730" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2667" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5732" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5622" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="5734" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5736" href="UALib.Algebras.Lifts.html#3828" class="Function">lift-alg</a> <a id="5745" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5709" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5747" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5608" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="5749" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2667" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5751" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5603" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="5753" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5622" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

-------------------------------

#### <a id="closure-properties">Closure properties</a>

The types defined above represent operators with useful closure properties. We now prove a handful of such properties since we will need them later.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="6692" class="Comment">-- P is a closure operator; in particular, it&#39;s expansive.</a>
<a id="P-expa"></a><a id="6751" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6751" class="Function">P-expa</a> <a id="6758" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6760" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6761" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6761" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="6763" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6765" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="6773" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="6775" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6775" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="6777" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6779" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="6784" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6785" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="6793" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6761" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="6795" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="6796" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="6798" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1698" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="6801" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6761" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6802" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="6805" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6807" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6775" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="6809" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2949" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="6811" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4328" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="6812" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6813" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6761" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6814" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="6816" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6761" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6817" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6819" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6775" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
<a id="6821" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6751" class="Function">P-expa</a><a id="6827" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6828" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6828" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6829" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="6831" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6831" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="6832" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6834" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6835" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6835" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="6836" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6838" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6838" class="Bound">KA</a> <a id="6841" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6843" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4791" class="InductiveConstructor">pisou</a><a id="6848" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6849" class="Argument">𝑨</a> <a id="6851" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6853" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6854" href="UALib.Algebras.Lifts.html#3828" class="Function">lift-alg</a> <a id="6863" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6835" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="6865" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6828" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6866" class="Symbol">)}{</a><a id="6869" class="Argument">𝑩</a> <a id="6871" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6873" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6835" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="6874" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6876" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6877" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4423" class="InductiveConstructor">pbase</a> <a id="6883" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6838" class="Bound">KA</a><a id="6885" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6887" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6888" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2380" class="Function">sym-≅</a> <a id="6894" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4327" class="Function">lift-alg-≅</a><a id="6904" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="6907" class="Comment">-- P is a closure operator; in particular, it&#39;s idempotent.</a>

<a id="7467" class="Comment">-- S is a closure operator; in particular, it&#39;s monotone.</a>

<a id="7867" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7525" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="7874" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7874" class="Bound">ante</a> <a id="7879" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7880" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3904" class="InductiveConstructor">siso</a> <a id="7885" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7885" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7887" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7887" class="Bound">x₁</a><a id="7889" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7891" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7893" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3904" class="InductiveConstructor">siso</a> <a id="7898" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7899" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7525" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="7906" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7874" class="Bound">ante</a> <a id="7911" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7885" class="Bound">x</a><a id="7912" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7914" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7887" class="Bound">x₁</a>

</pre>

We sometimes want to go back and forth between our two representations of subalgebras of algebras in a class. The tools `subalgebra→S` and `S→subalgebra` are made for that purpose.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="subalgebra→S"></a><a id="8126" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8126" class="Function">subalgebra→S</a> <a id="8139" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8141" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8142" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8142" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="8144" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8144" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="8146" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8148" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="8156" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="8158" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8158" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="8160" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8162" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="8167" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8168" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="8176" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8142" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="8178" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="8179" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="8181" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1698" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="8184" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8142" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="8185" class="Symbol">)}</a>
               <a id="8203" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8204" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8204" class="Bound">𝑪</a> <a id="8206" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8208" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="8216" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8217" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8142" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="8219" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="8221" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8144" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="8222" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8224" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="8225" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8227" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8229" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8204" class="Bound">𝑪</a> <a id="8231" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2044" class="Function Operator">IsSubalgebraOfClass</a> <a id="8251" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8158" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

  <a id="9887" class="Keyword">where</a>
   <a id="9896" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9896" class="Function">AS</a> <a id="9899" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9901" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9870" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="9903" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2044" class="Function Operator">IsSubalgebraOfClass</a> <a id="9923" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8617" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

   <a id="9997" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9997" class="Function">A≅SA</a> <a id="10002" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10004" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9870" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="10006" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#861" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="10008" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10371" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="10010" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9952" class="Function">SA</a> <a id="10013" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10371" class="Function Operator">∣</a>
   <a id="10018" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9997" class="Function">A≅SA</a> <a id="10023" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10025" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10456" class="Function">snd</a> <a id="10029" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10452" class="Function Operator">∥</a> <a id="10031" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10456" class="Function">snd</a> <a id="10035" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9896" class="Function">AS</a> <a id="10038" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10452" class="Function Operator">∥</a>

</pre>

Next we observe that lifting to a higher universe does not break the property of being a subalgebra of an algebra of a class.  In other words, if we lift a subalgebra of an algebra in a class, the result is still a subalgebra of an algebra in the class.

<pre class="Agda">

The next lemma would be too obvoius to care about were it not for the fact that we'll need it later, so it too must be formalized.

<pre class="Agda">

  <a id="12937" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12937" class="Function">lA≅B</a> <a id="12942" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12944" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12627" class="Function">lA</a> <a id="12947" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#861" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="12949" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12567" class="Bound">𝑩</a>
  <a id="12953" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12937" class="Function">lA≅B</a> <a id="12958" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="12960" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3811" class="Function">Trans-≅</a> <a id="12968" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12627" class="Function">lA</a> <a id="12971" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12567" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="12973" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12974" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2380" class="Function">sym-≅</a> <a id="12980" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4327" class="Function">lift-alg-≅</a><a id="12990" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12992" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12582" class="Bound">A≅B</a>

</pre>

We need to formalize one more lemma before arriving the short term objective of this section, which is the proof of the inclusion PS⊆SP.

<pre class="Agda">

class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="14082" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="14084" class="Argument">𝓘</a> <a id="14086" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14088" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13437" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="14089" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14091" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13443" class="Bound">hfe</a> <a id="14095" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13443"     <a id="14137" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14137" class="Function">iii</a> <a id="14141" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14143" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Basic.html#2093" class="Function">is-homomorphism</a> <a id="14159" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14160" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#678" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="14162" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13545" class="Function">SA</a><a id="14164" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14166" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14167" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#678" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="14169" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13500" class="Function">𝒜</a><a id="14170" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14172" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13971" class="Function">i</a>
    <a id="14178" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14137" class="Function">iii</a> <a id="14182" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14184" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="14186" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14186" class="Bound">𝑓</a> <a id="14188" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14188" class="Bound">𝒂</a> <a id="14190" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14192" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2277" class="Bound">gfe</a> <a id="14196" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="14198" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14198" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="14200" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14202" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14203" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10456" class="Function">snd</a> <a id="14207" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10452" class="Function Operator">∥</a> <a id="14209" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13782" class="Function">SA≤𝒜</a> <a id="14214" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14198" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="14216" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10452" class="Function Operator">∥</a><a id="14217" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14219" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14186" class="Bound">𝑓</a> <a id="14221" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="14224" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14224" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14226" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14228" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14188" class="Bound">𝒂</a> <a id="14230" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14224" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14232" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14198" class="Bound">i</a><a id="14233" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="14238" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14238" class="Function">ξ</a> <a id="14240" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14242" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#678" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="14244" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13500" class="Function">𝒜</a> <a id="14246" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2667" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="14248" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4328" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="14250" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13440" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
  <a id="14254" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14238" class="Function">ξ</a> <a id="14256" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14258" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4625" class="InductiveConstructor">produ</a><a id="14263" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14264" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13434" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="14265" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="14267" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13437" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="14268" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="14270" class="Argument">I</a> <a id="14272" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14274" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13448" class="Bound">I</a><a id="14275" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="14277" class="Argument">𝒜</a> <a id="14279" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14281" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13500" class="Function">𝒜</a><a id="14282" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14284" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="14287" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14287" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="14289" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14291" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6751" class="Function">P-expa</a> <a id="14298" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14299" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13600" class="Function">KA</a> <a id="14302" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14287" class="Bound">i</a><a id="14303" class="Symbol">))</a>

  <a id="14309" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14309" class="Function">γ</a> <a id="14311" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14313" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#678" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="14315" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13451" class="Bound">ℬ</a> <a id="14317" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#861" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="14319" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#678" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="14321" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13545" class="Function">SA</a>
  <a id="14326" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14309" class="Function">γ</a> <a id="14328" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14330" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#6161" class="Function">⨅≅</a> <a id="14333" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2277" class="Bound">gfe</a> <a id="14337" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13653" class="Function">B≅SA</a>

</pre>

#### PS(𝒦) ⊆ SP(𝒦)

Finally, we are in a position to prove that a product of subalgebras of algebras in a class 𝒦 is a subalgebra of a product of algebras in 𝒦.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="14531" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="14538" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14538" class="Module">_</a> <a id="14540" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14541" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14541" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="14543" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14545" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="14553" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="14555" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14555" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="14557" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14559" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="14564" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14565" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="14573" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14541" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="14575" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="14576" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="14578" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1698" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="14581" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14541" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="14582" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="14585" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14586" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14586" class="Bound">hfe</a> <a id="14590" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14592" href="MGS-FunExt-from-Univalence.html#2235" class="Function">hfunext</a> <a id="14600" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14601" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1698" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="14604" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14541" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="14605" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="14607" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1698" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="14610" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14541" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="14611" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="14614" class="Keyword">where</a>

#### <a id="more-class-inclusions">More class inclusions</a>

We conclude this module with three more inclusion relations that will have bit parts to play in our formal proof of Birkhoff's Theorem.

<a id="16831" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16564" class="Function">P⊆V</a> <a id="16835" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16836" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4791" class="InductiveConstructor">pisou</a> <a id="16842" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16842" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="16844" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16844" class="Bound">x₁</a><a id="16846" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16848" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="16850" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6283" class="InductiveConstructor">visou</a> <a id="16856" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16857" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16564" class="Function">P⊆V</a> <a id="16861" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16842" class="Bound">x</a><a id="16862" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16864" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16844" class="Bound">x₁</a>

<a id="SP⊆V"></a><a id="16904" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16904" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="16909" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16911" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16912" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16912" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="16914" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16914" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="16916" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16918" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="16926" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="16928" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16928" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="16930" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16932" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="16937" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16938" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="16946" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16912" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="16948" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="16949" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="16951" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1698" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="16954" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16912" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="16955" class="Symbol">)}</a>
 <a id="16959" class="Symbol">→</a>    <a id="16964" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3541" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="16965" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16966" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16912" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="16968" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="16970" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16914" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="16971" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="16973" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16912" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="16975" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="16977" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16914" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="16978" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16980" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16981" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4328" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="16982" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16983" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16912" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="16984" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="16986" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16914" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="16987" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16989" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16928" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="16990" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16992" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2949" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="16994" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5603" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="16995" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16996" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16912" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="16997" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="16999" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16914" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="17000" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17002" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16928" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
<a id="17004" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16904" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="17009" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17010" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3639" class="InductiveConstructor">sbase</a><a id="17015" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17016" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17016" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="17017" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17019" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17019" class="Bound">PCloA</a><a id="17024" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17026" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17028" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16564" class="Function">P⊆V</a> <a id="17032" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17033" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4871" class="InductiveConstructor">pisow</a> <a id="17039" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17019" class="Bound">PCloA</a> <a id="17045" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4327" class="Function">lift-alg-≅</a><a id="17055" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="17057" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16904" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="17062" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17063" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3696" class="InductiveConstructor">slift</a><a id="17068" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17069" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17069" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="17070" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17072" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17072" class="Bound">x</a><a id="17073" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17075" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17077" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5823" class="InductiveConstructor">vliftw</a> <a id="17084" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17085" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16904" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="17090" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17072" class="Bound">x</a><a id="17091" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="17214" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16904" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="17219" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17220" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3904" class="InductiveConstructor">siso</a> <a id="17225" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17225" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="17227" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17227" class="Bound">x₁</a><a id="17229" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17231" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17233" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6363" class="InductiveConstructor">visow</a> <a id="17239" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17240" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16904" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="17245" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17225" class="Bound">x</a><a id="17246" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17248" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17227" class="Bound">x₁</a>

</pre>


#### <a id="products-of-classes">Products of classes</a>

Above we proved PS(𝒦) ⊆ SP(𝒦).  It is slightly more painful to prove that the product of *all* algebras in the class S(𝒦) is a member of SP(𝒦). That is, ⨅ S(𝒦) ∈ SP(𝒦). This is mainly due to the fact that it's not obvious (at least not to this author-coder) what should be the type of the product of all members of a class of algebras.  After a few false starts, eventually the right type revealed itself.  Of course, now that we have it in our hands, it seems rather obvious.

We now describe the this type of product of all algebras in an arbitrary class 𝒦 of algebras of the same signature.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="17932" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="class-product"></a><a id="17939" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17939" class="Module">class-product</a> <a id="17953" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17954" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17954" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="17956" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17958" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="17966" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="17968" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17968" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="17970" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17972" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="17977" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17978" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="17986" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17954" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="17988" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="17989" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="17991" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1698" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="17994" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17954" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="17995" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="17998" class="Keyword">where</a>

 <a id="18006" class="Comment">-- ℑ serves as an index for the class</a>
 <a id="class-product.ℑ"></a><a id="18045" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18045" class="Function">ℑ</a> <a id="18047" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18049" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18050" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18050" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18052" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18054" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="18062" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18064" class="Symbol">→</a>  <a id="18067" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="18072" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18073" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="18081" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18050" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18083" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="18084" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="18086" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1698" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18089" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18050" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18090" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18092" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18094" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18095" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1698" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18098" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18050" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18099" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18101" href="universes.html#758" class="Function Operator">̇</a>
 <a id="18104" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18045" class="Function">ℑ</a> <a id="18106" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18107" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18107" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18108" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18110" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18110" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="18112" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18114" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">Σ</a> <a id="18116" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18116" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="18118" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">꞉</a> <a id="18120" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18121" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="18129" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18107" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18131" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="18132" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18134" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">,</a> <a id="18136" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18116" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="18138" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2667" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="18140" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18110" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

  <a id="18145" class="Comment">-- 𝔄 produces an algebra for each index (i : ℑ).</a>
 <a id="class-product.𝔄"></a><a id="18195" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18195" class="Function">𝔄</a> <a id="18197" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18199" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18200" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18200" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18202" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18204" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="18212" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="18214" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18214" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="18216" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18218" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="18223" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18224" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="18232" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18200" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18234" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="18235" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="18237" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1698" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18240" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18200" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18241" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="18244" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18246" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18045" class="Function">ℑ</a> <a id="18248" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18214" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="18250" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18252" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="18260" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18200" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18262" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a>
 <a id="18265" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18195" class="Function">𝔄</a><a id="18266" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18267" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18267" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18268" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="18270" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18270" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="18271" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18273" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18275" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="18277" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18278" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18278" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="18280" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18282" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18283" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18045" class="Function">ℑ</a> <a id="18285" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18270" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="18286" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="18289" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18291" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10371" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="18293" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18278" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="18295" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10371" class="Function Operator">∣</a>

 <a id="18299" class="Comment">-- The product of all members of 𝒦 can be written simply as follows:</a>
 <a id="class-product.class-product"></a><a id="18369" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18369" class="Function">class-product</a> <a id="18383" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18385" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18386" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18386" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18388" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18390" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="18398" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18400" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18402" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="18407" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18408" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="18416" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18386" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18418" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="18419" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="18421" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1698" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18424" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18386" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18425" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18427" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18429" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="18437" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18438" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1698" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18441" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18386" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18442" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18444" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a>
 <a id="18447" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18369" class="Function">class-product</a> <a id="18461" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18462" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18462" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18463" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18465" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18465" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="18467" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18469" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#678" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="18471" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="18473" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18195" class="Function">𝔄</a><a id="18474" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18475" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18462" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18476" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="18478" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18465" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="18479" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18481" class="Symbol">)</a>

 <a id="18485" class="Comment">-- ...or, more explicitly, here is the expansion of this indexed product.</a>
 <a id="class-product.class-product&#39;"></a><a id="18560" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18560" class="Function">class-product&#39;</a> <a id="18575" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18577" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18578" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18578" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18580" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18582" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="18590" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18592" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18594" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="18599" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18600" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="18608" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18578" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18610" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="18611" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="18613" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1698" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18616" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18578" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18617" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18619" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18621" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="18629" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18630" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1698" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18633" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18578" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18634" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18636" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a>
 <a id="18639" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18560" class="Function">class-product&#39;</a><a id="18653" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18654" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18654" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18655" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18657" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18657" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="18659" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18661" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#678" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="18663" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="18665" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18666" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18666" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="18668" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18670" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18671" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">Σ</a> <a id="18673" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18673" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="18675" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">꞉</a> <a id="18677" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18678" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="18686" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18654" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18688" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="18689" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18691" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">,</a> <a id="18693" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18673" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="18695" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2667" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="18697" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18657" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="18698" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="18701" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18703" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10371" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="18705" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18666" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="18707" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10371" class="Function Operator">∣</a>

</pre>

Notice that, if `p : 𝑨 ∈ 𝒦`, then we can think of the pair `(𝑨 , p) ∈ ℑ 𝒦` as an index over the class, and so we can think of `𝔄 (𝑨 , p)` (which is obviously `𝑨`) as the projection of the product `⨅ ( 𝔄{𝓤}{𝒦} )` onto the `(𝑨 , p)`-th component.

#### ⨅ S(𝒦) ∈ SP(𝒦)
Finally, we prove the result that plays a leading role in the formal proof of Birkhoff's Theorem---namely, that our newly defined class product ⨅ ( 𝔄{𝓤}{𝒦} ) belongs to SP(𝒦).

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="19179" class="Comment">-- The product of all subalgebras of a class 𝒦 belongs to SP(𝒦).</a>

   <a id="19808" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19808" class="Function">psPllA</a> <a id="19815" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19817" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#678" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="19819" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19554" class="Function">llA</a> <a id="19823" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2667" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="19825" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4328" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="19827" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19828" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3541" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="19830" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19292" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="19831" class="Symbol">)</a>
   <a id="19836" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19808" class="Function">psPllA</a> <a id="19843" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19845" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4625" class="InductiveConstructor">produ</a><a id="19850" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19851" class="Argument">𝓤</a> <a id="19853" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19855" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19856" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19364" class="Function">𝓸𝓿𝓾</a><a id="19859" class="Symbol">)}{</a><a id="19862" class="Argument">𝓦</a> <a id="19864" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19866" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19867" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19364" class="Function">𝓸𝓿𝓾</a><a id="19870" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="19873" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19723" class="Function">psllA</a>

   <a id="19883" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19883" class="Function">llA≅A</a> <a id="19889" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19891" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="19893" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19893" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="19895" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19897" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19898" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19554" class="Function">llA</a> <a id="19902" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19893" class="Bound">i</a><a id="19903" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19905" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#861" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="19907" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19908" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18195" class="Function">𝔄</a> <a id="19910" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19893" class="Bound">i</a><a id="19911" class="Symbol">)</a>
   <a id="19916" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19883" class="Function">llA≅A</a> <a id="19922" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19922" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="19924" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19926" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3811" class="Function">Trans-≅</a> <a id="19934" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19935" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19554" class="Function">llA</a> <a id="19939" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19922" class="Bound">i</a><a id="19940" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19942" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19943" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18195" class="Function">𝔄</a> <a id="19945" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19922" class="Bound">i</a><a id="19946" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19948" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19949" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2380" class="Function">sym-≅</a> <a id="19955" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4327" class="Function">lift-alg-≅</a><a id="19965" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19967" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19968" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2380" class="Function">sym-≅</a> <a id="19974" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4327" class="Function">lift-alg-≅</a><a id="19984" class="Symbol">)</a>

 <a id="19988" class="Comment">-- So, since PS⊆SP, we see that that the product of all subalgebras of a class 𝒦 belongs to SP(𝒦).</a>
 <a id="class-product-inclusions.class-prod-s-∈-sp"></a><a id="20088" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20088" class="Function">class-prod-s-∈-sp</a> <a id="20106" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20108" href="MGS-FunExt-from-Univalence.html#2235" class="Function">hfunext</a><a id="20115" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20116" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19364" class="Function">𝓸𝓿𝓾</a><a id="20119" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="20121" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19364" class="Function">𝓸𝓿𝓾</a><a id="20124" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20126" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20128" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18369" class="Function">class-product</a> <a id="20142" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20143" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3541" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="20145" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19292" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="20146" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20148" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2667" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="20150" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3541" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="20151" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20152" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4328" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="20154" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19292" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="20155" class="Symbol">)</a>
 <a id="20158" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20088" class="Function">class-prod-s-∈-sp</a> <a id="20176" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20176" class="Bound">hfe</a> <a id="20180" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="20182" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14651" class="Function">PS⊆SP</a><a id="20187" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20188" class="Argument">hfe</a> <a id="20192" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="20194" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20176" class="Bound">hfe</a><a id="20197" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20199" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19393" class="Function">class-prod-s-∈-ps</a>
